A server shall always start the default diagnostic session when powered up. If no other diagnostic session is started, then the default diagnostic session shall be running as long as the server is powered.魹ｽ
session_01魹ｽdefaultSession魹ｽ  魹ｽ` 魹ｽ魹ｽ魹ｽ魹ｽ魹ｽ魹ｽ This diagnosticSession is used to enable timed diagnostic service functionality (e.g., I/O control). The diagnostic functionality in this session shall also include all supported diagnostic functionality supported in the defaultSession.魹ｽ
